  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型能以端到端方式直接从视觉观测生成多模态机器人轨迹，但受限于离线数据集覆盖，遇到新环境时往往受到分布偏移影响，表现下降，甚至在安全性方面出现关键失误。约束在于，针对扩散模型进行强化学习适应有技术难度（如反向传播困难、值网络训练不稳定且高计算消耗）。

Method: 方法提出了结合扩散模型的多轨迹采样机制和Group Relative Policy Optimization（GRPO）策略，通过对采样轨迹间的相对优势进行估计，无需训练额外的值网络。同时，为兼顾预训练特征与新环境适应，仅微调高层decoder与action head，冻结视觉编码器，通过在线环境反馈增强安全性。

Result: 在Isaac Sim的PointGoal任务上，方法将成功率从52.0%提升到58.7%，路径得分（SPL）从0.49提升到0.54，并减少了碰撞事故。在真实四足机器人和几何分布外环境上，策略实现了零样本迁移，仍保持稳定性能。

Conclusion: 该强化学习微调框架显著提升了扩散模型导航策略在新环境下的适应性与安全泛化能力，为实际部署提供了更可靠的端到端解决方案。

Abstract: Diffusion-based robot navigation policies trained on large-scale imitation learning datasets, can generate multi-modal trajectories directly from the robot's visual observations, bypassing the traditional localization-mapping-planning pipeline and achieving strong zero-shot generalization. However, their performance remains constrained by the coverage of offline datasets, and when deployed in unseen settings, distribution shift often leads to accumulated trajectory errors and safety-critical failures. Adapting diffusion policies with reinforcement learning is challenging because their iterative denoising structure hinders effective gradient backpropagation, while also making the training of an additional value network computationally expensive and less stable. To address these issues, we propose a reinforcement learning fine-tuning framework tailored for diffusion-based navigation. The method leverages the inherent multi-trajectory sampling mechanism of diffusion models and adopts Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), which estimates relative advantages across sampled trajectories without requiring a separate value network. To preserve pretrained representations while enabling adaptation, we freeze the visual encoder and selectively update the higher decoder layers and action head, enhancing safety-aware behaviors through online environmental feedback. On the PointGoal task in Isaac Sim, our approach improves the Success Rate from 52.0% to 58.7% and SPL from 0.49 to 0.54 on unseen scenes, while reducing collision frequency. Additional experiments show that the fine-tuned policy transfers zero-shot to a real quadruped platform and maintains stable performance in geometrically out-of-distribution environments, suggesting improved adaptability and safe generalization to new domains.

*Jinwen Zhu,Xudong Zhao,Fangcheng Zhu,Jun Hu,Shi Jin,Yinian Mao,Guoquan Huang*

However, most state-of-the-art (SOTA) LiDAR-Inertial Odometry (LIO) systems still suffer from estimation inconsistency and computational bottlenecks when deployed on such platforms. To address these issues, this paper proposes a consistent and efficient tightly-coupled LIO framework tailored for UAVs. Within the efficient Multi-State Constraint Kalman Filter (MSCKF) framework, we build coplanar constraints inferred from planar features observed across a sliding window. By applying null-space projection to sliding-window coplanar constraints, we eliminate the direct dependency on feature parameters in the state vector, thereby mitigating overconfidence and improving consistency. More importantly, to further boost the efficiency, we introduce a parallel voxel-based data association and a novel compact cluster-to-plane measurement model. This compact measurement model losslessly reduces observation dimensionality and significantly accelerating the update process. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that our method outperforms most state-of-the-art (SOTA) approaches by providing a superior balance of consistency and efficiency. It exhibits improved robustness in degenerate scenarios, achieves the lowest memory usage via its map-free nature, and runs in real-time on resource-constrained embedded platforms (e.g., NVIDIA Jetson TX2).

### [183] [GoalSwarm: Multi-UAV Semantic Coordination for Open-Vocabulary Object Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12908)
*MoniJesu Wonders James,Amir Atef Habel,Aleksey Fedoseev,Dzmitry Tsetserokou*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了GoalSwarm框架，实现了多无人机在未知环境下的去中心化开集语义目标导航，不依赖重型模型即可协同完成目标物体搜索和定位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在未知环境中，无人机团队需要通过合作实现指定目标的定位和导航，但受限于设备计算性能、去中心化协同复杂性及对开放目标词的适应能力，现有方法难以广泛应用。

Method: GoalSwarm将多机间的观测深度信息实时投影构建2D语义占据图，避免了完整3D建模的高负载；集成了零样本基础模型SAM3以实现无需特定任务训练的像素级目标检测；通过贝叶斯价值映射融合多点观测置信度，并基于UCB原则指引前沿探索；采用去中心化招投标策略结合路径代价及空间分离惩罚，减少重叠探索。

Result: 实验表明，GoalSwarm能够高效、去中心化地实现开放词汇的目标导航，同时减轻了单机计算负担，实现了多无人机间的有效协作和任务分配。

Abstract: Cooperative visual semantic navigation is a foundational capability for aerial robot teams operating in unknown environments. However, achieving robust open-vocabulary object-goal navigation remains challenging due to the computational constraints of deploying heavy perception models onboard and the complexity of decentralized multi-agent coordination. We present GoalSwarm, a fully decentralized multi-UAV framework for zero-shot semantic object-goal navigation. Each UAV collaboratively constructs a shared, lightweight 2D top-down semantic occupancy map by projecting depth observations from aerial vantage points, eliminating the computational burden of full 3D representations while preserving essential geometric and semantic structure. The core contributions of GoalSwarm are threefold: (1) integration of zero-shot foundation model -- SAM3 for open vocabulary detection and pixel-level segmentation, enabling open-vocabulary target identification without task-specific training; (2) a Bayesian Value Map that fuses multi-viewpoint detection confidences into a per-pixel goal-relevance distribution, enabling informed frontier scoring via Upper Confidence Bound (UCB) exploration; and (3) a decentralized coordination strategy combining semantic frontier extraction, cost-utility bidding with geodesic path costs, and spatial separation penalties to minimize redundant exploration across the swarm.

### [184] [MotionAnymesh: Physics-Grounded Articulation for Simulation-Ready Digital Twins](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12936)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有零样本方法在将3D网格转为可交互资产时，常因缺乏物理约束而产生运动学幻觉及网格穿透问题，影响后续AI与机器人仿真。迫切需要结合物理知识，提高转换后资产质量。

Abstract: Converting static 3D meshes into interactable articulated assets is crucial for embodied AI and robotic simulation. However, existing zero-shot pipelines struggle with complex assets due to a critical lack of physical grounding. Specifically, ungrounded Vision-Language Models (VLMs) frequently suffer from kinematic hallucinations, while unconstrained joint estimation inevitably leads to catastrophic mesh inter-penetration during physical simulation. ### [185] [RoboStream: Weaving Spatio-Temporal Reasoning with Memory in Vision-Language Models for Robotics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12939)
*Yuzhi Huang,Jie Wu,Weijue Bu,Ziyi Xiong,Gaoyang Jiang,Ye Li,Kangye Ji,Shuzhao Xie,Yue Huang,Chenglei Wu,Jingyan Jiang,Zhi Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 现有VLM方法长时序机器人操作表现差，其缺乏空间-时间推理和因果记忆。本文提出RoboStream框架，通过空间-时间融合令牌和因果图实现几何锚定和记忆，无需训练即可大幅提升任务表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前VLM驱动的机器人规划系统在长时序任务中易丢失场景状态，无法追踪遮挡或动作结果，导致操作失败。而人类则能持续追踪空间关系，并记忆动作影响。这一差距限制了机器人在开放世界的应用。

Method: 提出RoboStream：1）空间-时间融合令牌（STF-Tokens）绑定视觉证据和3D属性，实现对象锚定与记忆；2）因果空间-时间图（CSTG）记录跨步骤的状态变化，追踪因果链。整个系统无需额外训练。

Result: 在长时序RLBench任务中RoboStream达到90.5%的成功率，在真实世界堆积方块任务中达到44.4%；而SOTA如SoFar与VoxPoser仅得11.1%。

Conclusion: 空间-时间推理与因果记忆对于机器人长时序操作至关重要，RoboStream无需训练即可显著提升表现，为通用机器人智能奠定基础。

Abstract: Enabling reliable long-horizon robotic manipulation is a crucial step toward open-world embodied intelligence. However, VLM-based planners treat each step as an isolated observation-to-action mapping, forcing them to reinfer scene geometry from raw pixels at every decision point while remaining unaware of how prior actions have reshaped the environment. Despite strong short-horizon performance, these systems lack the spatio-temporal reasoning required for persistent geometric anchoring and memory of action-triggered state transitions. Without persistent state tracking, perceptual errors accumulate across the execution horizon, temporarily occluded objects are catastrophically forgotten, and these compounding failures lead to precondition violations that cascade through subsequent steps. In contrast, humans maintain a persistent mental model that continuously tracks spatial relations and action consequences across interactions rather than reconstructing them at each instant. Inspired by this human capacity for causal spatio-temporal reasoning with persistent memory, we propose RoboStream, a training-free framework that achieves geometric anchoring through Spatio-Temporal Fusion Tokens (STF-Tokens), which bind visual evidence to 3D geometric attributes for persistent object grounding, and maintains causal continuity via a Causal Spatio-Temporal Graph (CSTG) that records action-triggered state transitions across steps. This design enables the planner to trace causal chains and preserve object permanence under occlusion without additional training or fine-tuning. RoboStream achieves 90.5% on long-horizon RLBench and 44.4% on challenging real-world block-building tasks, where both SoFar and VoxPoser score 11.1%, demonstrating that spatio-temporal reasoning and causal memory are critical missing components for reliable long-horizon manipulation.

</details>


### [186] [Coordinated Manipulation of Hybrid Deformable-Rigid Objects in Constrained Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12940)
*Anees Peringal,Anup Teejo Mathew,Panagiotis liatsis,Federico Renda*

Main category: cs.RO

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，机器人操作可变形线性物体（如绳索、缆绳）已有大量研究，但面对同时包含刚性和可变形元素的混合体（如部分刚性、部分柔性结构）以及受限制的空间环境，依然存在很大挑战。本研究旨在解决这些复杂操作场景下的策略规划难题。

Method: 论文提出采用基于应变的Cosserat杆模型，将刚体操作理论推广至混合可变形线性对象（hDLO）。通过可微分物理模型及解析梯度，先求解逆静力学（IKS）问题并作为轨迹优化的初始解，从而实现高效规划，并显著加快求解速度（比有限差分法快33倍）。

Result: 所提算法经仿真与实际实验（包括双臂机器人操控三连杆hDLO）验证，操作精度高，平均变形误差仅约为3厘米（占可变形部分长度的5%）。与基于采样的可行性规划器对比，提出方法在精度与效率上均有显著提升。

Conclusion: 该方法能够高效且准确地在受限环境中控制混合刚-柔线性物体，推动机器人操作在复杂装配和受限空间场景中的应用。

Abstract: Coordinated robotic manipulation of deformable linear objects (DLOs), such as ropes and cables, has been widely studied; however, handling hybrid assemblies composed of both deformable and rigid elements in constrained environments remains challenging. This work presents a quasi-static optimization-based manipulation planner that employs a strain-based Cosserat rod model, extending rigid-body formulations to hybrid deformable linear objects (hDLO). The proposed planner exploits the compliance of deformable links to maneuver through constraints while achieving task-space objectives for the object that are unreachable with rigid tools. By leveraging a differentiable model with analytically derived gradients, the method achieves up to a 33x speedup over finite-difference baselines for inverse kinetostatic(IKS) problems. Furthermore, the subsequent trajectory optimization problem, warm-started using the IKS solution, is only practically realizable via analytical derivatives. The proposed algorithm is validated in simulation on various hDLO systems and experimentally on a three-link hDLO manipulated in a constrained environment using a dual-arm robotic system. Experimental results confirm the planner's accuracy, yielding an average deformation error of approximately 3 cm (5% of the deformable link length) between the desired and measured marker positions. Finally, the proposed optimal planner is compared against a sampling-based feasibility planner adapted to the strain-based formulation. The results demonstrate the effectiveness and applicability of the proposed approach for robotic manipulation of hybrid assemblies in constrained environments.

### [187] [ReMem-VLA: Empowering Vision-Language-Action Model with Memory via Dual-Level Recurrent Queries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12942)
*Hang Li,Fengyi Shen,Dong Chen,Liudi Yang,Xudong Wang,Jinkui Shi,Zhenshan Bing,Ziyuan Liu,Alois Knoll*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文提出了ReMem-VLA模型，通过引入两类可学习查询机制，实现了视觉-语言-动作模型对短期和长期记忆的有效整合，大幅提升机器人在需要历史上下文的任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言-动作闭环控制模型通常假定每个状态只依赖当前观测（Markov假设），但这会导致模型在需要历史信息的任务中表现不佳。以往的记忆机制或容易被干扰项误导，或记忆窗口有限，难以长期保留关键信息。

Method: 提出了ReMem-VLA模型，采用两类可学习记忆查询：帧级查询实现连续帧间的信息传递用于短期记忆，分段级查询用于跨时间段传递上下文以支持长期记忆，同时引入了历史观测预测作为辅助训练目标。模型端到端训练，无额外推理负担。

Result: 通过大量基于记忆的仿真与真实机器人实验，ReMem-VLA在空间、顺序、情节、时间以及视觉记忆维度上均表现出强大的记忆能力，显著优于无记忆和主流带记忆的VLA基线，并在记忆依赖型任务中大幅提升表现。

Conclusion: ReMem-VLA有效解决了VLA模型在历史依赖任务中的记忆缺陷，兼具短期和长期记忆，提升了机器人在复杂任务中的决策和执行能力。

Abstract: Vision-language-action (VLA) models for closed-loop robot control are typically cast under the Markov assumption, making them prone to errors on tasks requiring historical context. To incorporate memory, existing VLAs either retrieve from a memory bank, which can be misled by distractors, or extend the frame window, whose fixed horizon still limits long-term retention. In this paper, we introduce ReMem-VLA, a Recurrent Memory VLA model equipped with two sets of learnable queries: frame-level recurrent memory queries for propagating information across consecutive frames to support short-term memory, and chunk-level recurrent memory queries for carrying context across temporal chunks for long-term memory. These queries are trained end-to-end to aggregate and maintain relevant context over time, implicitly guiding the model's decisions without additional training or inference cost. Furthermore, to enhance visual memory, we introduce Past Observation Prediction as an auxiliary training objective. Through extensive memory-centric simulation and real-world robot experiments, we demonstrate that ReMem-VLA exhibits strong memory capabilities across multiple dimensions, including spatial, sequential, episodic, temporal, and visual memory. ReMem-VLA significantly outperforms memory-free VLA baselines $π$0.5 and OpenVLA-OFT and surpasses MemoryVLA on memory-dependent tasks by a large margin.

### [188] [Efficient Real-World Autonomous Racing via Attenuated Residual Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12960)
*Raphael Trumpp,Denis Hoornaert,Mirco Theile,Marco Caccamo*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为α-RPO（Attenuated Residual Policy Optimization）的新方法，旨在解决残差策略学习（RPL）在实际机器人部署中系统复杂性高和推理延迟大的问题。该方法通过渐进式弱化初始基准策略影响，最终得到端到端的神经网络策略，并在仿真和实车测试中实现了更高效且表现更优的自动驾驶。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RPL虽然能够利用深度强化学习提升机器人任务表现（如自动驾赛车），但其部署时需要同时运行基础策略和神经网络残差，带来系统复杂度和响应延迟的问题。为便于在真实机器人上应用，亟需一种降低复杂度且不损失性能的改进方法。

Method: 引入α-RPO方法，训练初期让基准策略主导学习，随着训练的递进逐步减少（Attenuate）基准策略的影响，最终神经网络可以独立决策。方法可与PPO等主流RL算法无缝集成，同时允许初始基准策略使用一些最终部署不需要的感知信号，提升了训练阶段效率。

Result: 基于α-RPO构建了1:10尺度的自动驾驶竞速框架，并在仿真和实车（Roboracer）场景下进行了测试。结果表明：与传统RPL及其他基线相比，该方法大幅降低了系统复杂度，同时车辆的驾驶表现得到提升，且具备更好的零样本迁移能力。

Conclusion: α-RPO创新性地解决了RPL部署系统复杂和延迟高的难题，不仅简化了真实机器人系统，也提升了控制性能，为高效落地DRL控制器提供了新的解决思路和实证依据。

Abstract: Residual policy learning (RPL), in which a learned policy refines a static base policy using deep reinforcement learning (DRL), has shown strong performance across various robotic applications. Its effectiveness is particularly evident in autonomous racing, a domain that serves as a challenging benchmark for real-world DRL. However, deploying RPL-based controllers introduces system complexity and increases inference latency. We address this by introducing an extension of RPL named attenuated residual policy optimization ($α$-RPO). Unlike standard RPL, $α$-RPO yields a standalone neural policy by progressively attenuating the base policy, which initially serves to bootstrap learning. Furthermore, this mechanism enables a form of privileged learning, where the base policy is permitted to use sensor modalities not required for final deployment. We design $α$-RPO to integrate seamlessly with PPO, ensuring that the attenuated influence of the base controller is dynamically compensated during policy optimization. We evaluate $α$-RPO by building a framework for 1:10-scaled autonomous racing around it. In both simulation and zero-shot real-world transfer to Roboracer cars, $α$-RPO not only reduces system complexity but also improves driving performance compared to baselines - demonstrating its practicality for robotic deployment. Our code is available at: https://github.com/raphajaner/arpo_racing.

</details>

Method: LaDA框架利用自然语言作为语义桥梁，引入三类可解释的动作原语层（平移、旋转、夹爪控制）作为中介层，通过软标签对比学习对齐动作原语，并采用课程学习启发的自适应权重策略联合优化对比与模仿目标。

Abstract: The heterogeneity between high-level vision-language understanding and low-level action control remains a fundamental challenge in robotic manipulation. Although recent methods have advanced task-specific action alignment, they often struggle to generate robust and accurate actions for novel or semantically related tasks. To address this, we propose the Language-Grounded Decoupled Action Representation (LaDA) framework, which leverages natural language as a semantic bridge to connect perception and control. LaDA introduces a fine-grained intermediate layer of three interpretable action primitives--translation, rotation, and gripper control--providing explicit semantic structure for low-level actions. It further employs a semantic-guided soft-label contrastive learning objective to align similar action primitives across tasks, enhancing generalization and motion consistency. An adaptive weighting strategy, inspired by curriculum learning, dynamically balances contrastive and imitation objectives for stable and effective training. Extensive experiments on simulated benchmarks (LIBERO and MimicGen) and real-world demonstrations validate that LaDA achieves strong performance and generalizes effectively to unseen or related tasks.

In this work, two variants of the priority-based Fragment Planner (FP) are presented as resource-centric MRPP algorithms that leverage route fragmentation to enable partial route progression and limit the impact of binary-based waiting. Their performances are contrasted against 5 baseline algorithms with varying robotic fleet sizes. ### [191] [From Passive Monitoring to Active Defence: Resilient Control of Manipulators Under Cyberattacks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13003)
*Gabriele Gualandi,Alessandro V. Papadopoulos*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对冗余操作机械臂在面对隐蔽型伪数据注入攻击（FDIA）时的主动防御架构，通过控制输入动态调节，有效降低末端执行器偏差，同时保证正常任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的被动异常检测（如卡方检验）容易被隐蔽FDIA绕过，攻击者可以在不触发报警的情况下对机器人系统造成严重影响。因此，需要更主动的防御机制提升系统韧性。

Method: 作者构建了一个集成反馈线性化机械臂、稳态卡尔曼滤波器和卡方异常检测器的闭环模型。在此基础上，提出了一种基于全新预测器（无需测量投影于驱动空间）的主动防御方法，通过异常评分的单调函数对控制输入进行实时衰减，理论上保证执行损耗符合概率界且系统稳定。同时，从攻击者角度构建QCQP，分析最优隐蔽攻击。

Result: 在6自由度的平面机械臂仿真中，主动防御措施在遭受攻击时大幅降低了末端执行器的偏差，而在无攻击环境下基本不影响任务表现。

Conclusion: 该主动控制级防御架构显著提升了机械臂在面对隐蔽FDIA时的安全性和稳健性，兼顾了安全和正常操作需求。

Abstract: Cyber-physical robotic systems are vulnerable to false data injection attacks (FDIAs), in which an adversary corrupts sensor signals while evading residual-based passive anomaly detectors such as the chi-squared test. Such stealthy attacks can induce substantial end-effector deviations without triggering alarms. This paper studies the resilience of redundant manipulators to stealthy FDIAs and advances the architecture from passive monitoring to active defence. We formulate a closed-loop model comprising a feedback-linearized manipulator, a steady-state Kalman filter, and a chi-squared-based anomaly detector. Building on this passive monitoring layer, we propose an active control-level defence that attenuates the control input through a monotone function of an anomaly score generated by a novel actuation-projected, measurement-free state predictor. The proposed design provides probabilistic guarantees on nominal actuation loss and preserves closed-loop stability. From the attacker perspective, we derive a convex QCQP for computing one-step optimal stealthy attacks. Simulations on a 6-DOF planar manipulator show that the proposed defence significantly reduces attack-induced end-effector deviation while preserving nominal task performance in the absence of attacks.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者构建了SldprtNet数据集，采集了24.2万个工业零件，提供.step和.sldprt格式。开发了支持损失less转换的编码器和解码器系统，将3D模型与结构化文本及渲染图像结合。每个样本都有人工作对齐的自然语言描述。用Qwen2.5-VL-7B多模态模型生成并验证描述，并用基线模型在子集上进行多模态与单模态对比实验。

Result: 多模态输入（图像+文本）优于单文本输入，实验表明多模态数据对提升CAD模型生成效果具有不可或缺的价值。支持工具和描述数据完全对齐，保障了数据一致性和质量。

Conclusion: SldprtNet作为全对齐、多模态的大规模真实工业零件数据集，大大丰富了3D设计、语义CAD建模与跨模态学习的基础资源，并拓展了自动化CAD设计研究的可能性。

Abstract: We introduce SldprtNet, a large-scale dataset comprising over 242,000 industrial parts, designed for semantic-driven CAD modeling, geometric deep learning, and the training and fine-tuning of multimodal models for 3D design. The dataset provides 3D models in both .step and .sldprt formats to support diverse training and testing. To enable parametric modeling and facilitate dataset scalability, we developed supporting tools, an encoder and a decoder, which support 13 types of CAD commands and enable lossless transformation between 3D models and a structured text representation. Additionally, each sample is paired with a composite image created by merging seven rendered views from different viewpoints of the 3D model, effectively reducing input token length and accelerating inference. By combining this image with the parameterized text output from the encoder, we employ the lightweight multimodal language model Qwen2.5-VL-7B to generate a natural language description of each part's appearance and functionality. To ensure accuracy, we manually verified and aligned the generated descriptions, rendered images, and 3D models. These descriptions, along with the parameterized modeling scripts, rendered images, and 3D model files, are fully aligned to construct SldprtNet. To assess its effectiveness, we fine-tuned baseline models on a dataset subset, comparing image-plus-text inputs with text-only inputs. Results confirm the necessity and value of multimodal datasets for CAD generation. It features carefully selected real-world industrial parts, supporting tools for scalable dataset expansion, diverse modalities, and ensured diversity in model complexity and geometric features, making it a comprehensive multimodal dataset built for semantic-driven CAD modeling and cross-modal learning.

</details>


### [193] [Evaluating VLMs' Spatial Reasoning Over Robot Motion: A Step Towards Robot Planning with Motion Preferences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13100)
*Wenxi Wu,Jingjing Zhang,Martim Brandão*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文分析了四种先进的视觉-语言模型（VLM）在机器人运动空间推理任务中的表现，发现部分VLM具有潜力提升机器人规划的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大型基础模型已应用于任务规划，但其能否满足用户空间约束和偏好（如距离、拓扑属性或运动风格）尚不明确。作者希望揭示主流VLM的空间推理能力，以指引机器人任务规划的改进。

Method: 作者评估了四种前沿VLM（包括Qwen2.5-VL和GPT-4o），结合四种提问方法，对机器人运动中的空间推理进行实验，包括对象接近性和路径风格偏好，并对准确率和计算开销进行了综合分析。

Result: Qwen2.5-VL在零样本推理时达到71.4%的准确率，经微调的小模型提升到75%，而GPT-4o表现较弱。不同模型和提问方式在准确率与计算代价上有权衡。

Conclusion: 部分VLM具备与机器人运动规划集成的潜力，可用于实现用户空间偏好约束，但整体性能和代价权衡仍有提升空间。

Abstract: Understanding user instructions and object spatial relations in surrounding environments is crucial for intelligent robot systems to assist humans in various tasks. The natural language and spatial reasoning capabilities of Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have the potential to enhance the generalization of robot planners on new tasks, objects, and motion specifications. While foundation models have been applied to task planning, it is still unclear the degree to which they have the capability of spatial reasoning required to enforce user preferences or constraints on motion, such as desired distances from objects, topological properties, or motion style preferences. In this paper, we evaluate the capability of four state-of-the-art VLMs at spatial reasoning over robot motion, using four different querying methods. Our results show that, with the highest-performing querying method, Qwen2.5-VL achieves 71.4% accuracy zero-shot and 75% on a smaller model after fine-tuning, and GPT-4o leads to lower performance. We evaluate two types of motion preferences (object-proximity and path-style), and we also analyze the trade-off between accuracy and computation cost in number of tokens. This work shows some promise in the potential of VLM integration with robot motion planning pipelines.

</details>


### [194] [A Feasibility-Enhanced Control Barrier Function Method for Multi-UAV Collision Avoidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13103)
*Qishen Zhong,Junlong Wu,Jian Yang,Guanwei Xiao,Junqi Wu,Zimeng Jiang,Pingan Fang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种增强可行性的控制障碍函数（FECBF）框架，用于多无人机碰撞避免，在复杂场景下提升可行性和安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多无人机密集场景下，由于多个控制障碍函数（CBF）约束之间存在内部不兼容性，容易导致CBF二次规划（QP）问题不可行，影响安全性和控制效果。

Method: 本文分析了CBF约束的内部兼容性，给出了充分条件，并提出通过引入符号一致性约束来缓解不兼容问题。该约束结合最坏估计和松弛变量纳入分布式CBF-QP求解框架中。

Result: 仿真结果表明，该方法在密集场景下显著减少了不可行性，比现有方法具有更好的碰撞避免性能。在不同时间延迟下的仿真进一步证明了其鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该方法能有效增强多无人机系统碰撞避免的可行性和实用性，并且通过实际无人机实验验证了其实用价值。

Abstract: This paper presents a feasibility-enhanced control barrier function (FECBF) framework for multi-UAV collision avoidance. In dense multi-UAV scenarios, the feasibility of the CBF quadratic program (CBF-QP) can be compromised due to internal incompatibility among multiple CBF constraints. To address this issue, we analyze the internal compatibility of CBF constraints and derive a sufficient condition for internal compatibility. Based on this condition, a sign-consistency constraint is introduced to mitigate internal incompatibility. The proposed constraint is incorporated into a decentralized CBF-QP formulation using worst-case estimates and slack variables. Simulation results demonstrate that the proposed method significantly reduces infeasibility and improves collision avoidance performance compared with existing baselines in dense scenarios. Additional simulations under varying time delays demonstrate the robustness of the proposed method. Real-world experiments validate the practical applicability of the proposed method.

</details>


### [195] [Panoramic Multimodal Semantic Occupancy Prediction for Quadruped Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13108)
*Guoqiang Zhao,Zhe Yang,Sheng Wu,Fei Teng,Mengfei Duan,Yuanfan Zheng,Kai Luo,Kailun Yang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文针对四足机器人复杂环境下全景占据预测的问题，提出了首个真实场景下的全景多模态占据数据集PanoMMOcc，以及专为腿式机器人和球面成像设计的占据感知框架VoxelHound。该方法显著提升了三维占据预测的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的占据预测方法大多服务于轮式自动驾驶，依赖于RGB视觉信息，对于运动灵活、高动态视角变化的四足机器人在复杂环境下表现不佳，缺少针对多模态感知的公开数据集和系统方法，制约了四足移动机器人在 embodied 3D 感知领域的发展。

Method: 提出了PanoMMOcc数据集，包含四种传感器模态和多种复杂场景。提出VoxelHound感知框架，设计了垂直抖动补偿（VJC）模块来缓解机器人运动带来的强烈视角变化，并通过多模态信息融合（MIPF）模块有效融合全景视觉和辅助信息，实现精准的体素级三维占据预测。

Result: VOXELHOUND在PanoMMOcc基准上实现了最新的性能提升，mIoU提升4.16%，显著优于现有方法。数据集及代码工具开放，促进了系统评测和后续研究。

Conclusion: 本研究为四足机器人复杂场景下的全景多模态3D占据感知提供了从数据到方法的完整方案，提升了机器人的理解和适应能力，为未来embodied 3D感知和机器人导航等应用打下基础。

Abstract: Panoramic imagery provides holistic 360° visual coverage for perception in quadruped robots. However, existing occupancy prediction methods are mainly designed for wheeled autonomous driving and rely heavily on RGB cues, limiting their robustness in complex environments. To bridge this gap, (1) we present PanoMMOcc, the first real-world panoramic multimodal occupancy dataset for quadruped robots, featuring four sensing modalities across diverse scenes. (2) We propose a panoramic multimodal occupancy perception framework, VoxelHound, tailored for legged mobility and spherical imaging. Specifically, we design (i) a Vertical Jitter Compensation (VJC) module to mitigate severe viewpoint perturbations caused by body pitch and roll during mobility, enabling more consistent spatial reasoning, and (ii) an effective Multimodal Information Prompt Fusion (MIPF) module that jointly leverages panoramic visual cues and auxiliary modalities to enhance volumetric occupancy prediction. (3) We establish a benchmark based on PanoMMOcc and provide detailed data analysis to enable systematic evaluation of perception methods under challenging embodied scenarios. Extensive experiments demonstrate that VoxelHound achieves state-of-the-art performance on PanoMMOcc (+4.16%} in mIoU). The dataset and code will be publicly released to facilitate future research on panoramic multimodal 3D perception for embodied robotic systems at https://github.com/SXDR/PanoMMOcc, along with the calibration tools released at https://github.com/losehu/CameraLiDAR-Calib.

</details>


### [196] [DecoVLN: Decoupling Observation, Reasoning, and Correction for Vision-and-Language Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13133)
*Zihao Xin,Wentong Li,Yixuan Jiang,Bin Wang,Runming Cong,Jie Qin,Shengjun Huang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 论文提出了一个名为DecoVLN的新方法，用于解决视觉-语言导航中的长期记忆构建和累计误差两个关键问题，并在实际环境中验证了效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言导航（VLN）方法在长远程指令跟随和复杂环境导航中，长期记忆构建不理想且容易积累导航误差，影响整体性能。

Method: 1）将长期记忆构建建模为优化问题，引入统一打分函数，兼顾语义相关性、视觉多样性和历史轨迹的时间覆盖性，并采用自适应机制优化记忆帧；2）提出基于状态-动作对级别的修正规则，通过地理距离精准度量偏离，筛选高质量数据，提升误差修正的效率与稳定性。

Result: 大量实验表明，DecoVLN能有效提升导航鲁棒性，并已成功应用于真实世界环境。

Conclusion: DecoVLN针对VLN的长期记忆和累积误差两大瓶颈提出了有效的解决框架，显著增强了代理的导航能力和准确性。

Abstract: Vision-and-Language Navigation (VLN) requires agents to follow long-horizon instructions and navigate complex 3D environments. However, existing approaches face two major challenges: constructing an effective long-term memory bank and overcoming the compounding errors problem. To address these issues, we propose DecoVLN, an effective framework designed for robust streaming perception and closed-loop control in long-horizon navigation. First, we formulate long-term memory construction as an optimization problem and introduce adaptive refinement mechanism that selects frames from a historical candidate pool by iteratively optimizing a unified scoring function. This function jointly balances three key criteria: semantic relevance to the instruction, visual diversity from the selected memory, and temporal coverage of the historical trajectory. Second, to alleviate compounding errors, we introduce a state-action pair-level corrective finetuning strategy. By leveraging geodesic distance between states to precisely quantify deviation from the expert trajectory, the agent collects high-quality state-action pairs in the trusted region while filtering out the polluted data with low relevance. This improves both the efficiency and stability of error correction. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of DecoVLN, and we have deployed it in real-world environments.

</details>
